  Number of basis used : 0, 1 


  Optimal -> $$,  Semi-optimal -> ## 


  Rightmost explanation ->  Number of optimal basis , Semi-optimal sum 


  Bottom explanation ->  Optimal sum , semi-optimal sum 


  Use Percentage : 0 ~ 0.000000
